   255â†’
   256â†’            // Handle image content
   257â†’            for (const [filePath, content] of Object.entries(this.loadedContent)) {
   258â†’                if (filePath.match(/\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg)$/i)) {
   259â†’                    await this.injectImageContent(filePath, content);
   260â†’                }
   261â†’            }
   262â†’        }
   263â†’
   264â†’        /**
   265â†’         * Creates a virtual page navigation for Session 10
   266â†’         */
   267â†’
   268â†’        /**
   269â†’         * Replaces only the article content, preserving MkDocs navigation structure
   270â†’         */
   271â†’        async replacePageContent(markdownContent) {
   272â†’            try {
   273â†’                // Prevent duplicate content replacement
   274â†’                if (this._isReplacingContent) {
   275â†’                    console.log('ğŸ”„ Content replacement already in progress, skipping duplicate call');
   276â†’                    return;
   277â†’                }
   278â†’                this._isReplacingContent = true;
   279â†’                
   280â†’                // Target only the actual article content, not the entire content area
   281â†’                const selectors = [
   282â†’                    'article.md-typeset',                       // Direct article with content
   283â†’                    '.md-content__inner article',               // Article within content
   284â†’                    '.md-typeset > *',                          // Direct children of typeset
   285â†’                    '.md-content__inner .md-typeset'            // Fallback to typeset area
   286â†’                ];
   287â†’                
   288â†’                let contentArea = null;
   289â†’                for (const selector of selectors) {
   290â†’                    contentArea = document.querySelector(selector);
   291â†’                    if (contentArea) {
   292â†’                        console.log('âœ… Found content area using selector:', selector);
   293â†’                        break;
   294â†’                    }
   295â†’                }
   296â†’                
   297â†’                if (!contentArea) {
   298â†’                    console.error('âŒ Could not find any content area to replace');
   299â†’                    return;
   300â†’                }
   301â†’                
   302â†’                console.log('ğŸ”„ Replacing minimal content area:', contentArea.tagName);
   303â†’                
   304â†’                // First, replace image references with base64 data URLs
   305â†’                let processedContent = await this.replaceImagesWithBase64(markdownContent);
   306â†’                
   307â†’                // Enhanced markdown to HTML conversion with better structure handling
   308â†’                // IMPORTANT: Process images BEFORE links to avoid conflicts
   309â†’                let htmlContent = processedContent;
   310â†’                
   311â†’                // First handle code blocks to protect them from other processing
   312â†’                const codeBlocks = [];
   313â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, (match, lang, code) => {
   314â†’                    const index = codeBlocks.length;
   315â†’                    codeBlocks.push(`<pre><code class="language-${lang || ''}">${code.trim()}</code></pre>`);
   316â†’                    return `__CODE_BLOCK_${index}__`;
   317â†’                });
   318â†’                
   319â†’                // Handle headings with automatic ID generation for navigation and scroll highlighting
   320â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent
   321â†’                    .replace(/^# (.+)$/gm, (match, title) => {
   322â†’                        const id = this.generateHeadingId(title);
   323â†’                        return `<h1 id="${id}">${title}</h1>`;
   324â†’                    })
   325â†’                    .replace(/^## (.+)$/gm, (match, title) => {
   326â†’                        const id = this.generateHeadingId(title);
   327â†’                        return `<h2 id="${id}">${title}</h2>`;
   328â†’                    })
   329â†’                    .replace(/^### (.+)$/gm, (match, title) => {
   330â†’                        const id = this.generateHeadingId(title);
   331â†’                        return `<h3 id="${id}">${title}</h3>`;
   332â†’                    })
   333â†’                    .replace(/^#### (.+)$/gm, (match, title) => {
   334â†’                        const id = this.generateHeadingId(title);
   335â†’                        return `<h4 id="${id}">${title}</h4>`;
   336â†’                    })
   337â†’                    .replace(/^##### (.+)$/gm, (match, title) => {
   338â†’                        const id = this.generateHeadingId(title);
   339â†’                        return `<h5 id="${id}">${title}</h5>`;
   340â†’                    });
   341â†’                
   342â†’                // Handle text formatting
   343â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent
   344â†’                    .replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>')
   345â†’                    .replace(/\*([^*]+?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>')
   346â†’                    .replace(/`([^`]+?)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
   347â†’                
   348â†’                // Handle images and links (images first to avoid conflicts)
   349â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent
   350â†’                    .replace(/!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, '<img src="$2" alt="$1" style="max-width: 100%; height: auto;">')
   351â†’                    .replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, '<a href="$2">$1</a>');
   352â†’                
   353â†’                // Handle lists - improved handling
   354â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/^(\s*)-\s+(.+)$/gm, (match, indent, content) => {
   355â†’                    const level = Math.floor(indent.length / 2);
   356â†’                    return `<li data-level="${level}">${content}</li>`;
   357â†’                });
   358â†’                
   359â†’                // Wrap consecutive list items in ul tags
   360â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/(<li[^>]*>.*?<\/li>\s*)+/gs, (match) => {
   361â†’                    return `<ul>${match}</ul>`;
   362â†’                });
   363â†’                
   364â†’                // Handle numbered lists
   365â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(/^(\s*)\d+\.\s+(.+)$/gm, (match, indent, content) => {
   366â†’                    const level = Math.floor(indent.length / 2);
   367â†’                    return `<li data-level="${level}">${content}</li>`;
   368â†’                });
   369â†’                
   370â†’                // Convert paragraphs - be more careful about existing HTML
   371â†’                const lines = htmlContent.split('\n');
   372â†’                let inList = false;
   373â†’                let result = [];
   374â†’                
   375â†’                for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
   376â†’                    const line = lines[i].trim();
   377â†’                    
   378â†’                    if (!line) {
   379â†’                        result.push('');
   380â†’                        continue;
   381â†’                    }
   382â†’                    
   383â†’                    // Check if line is already HTML
   384â†’                    if (line.startsWith('<') || line.includes('__CODE_BLOCK_')) {
   385â†’                        result.push(line);
   386â†’                        inList = line.includes('<li') || line.includes('<ul') || line.includes('<ol');
   387â†’                    } else if (!inList) {
   388â†’                        // Only wrap in paragraph if not already HTML and not in a list
   389â†’                        result.push(`<p>${line}</p>`);
   390â†’                    } else {
   391â†’                        result.push(line);
   392â†’                    }
   393â†’                }
   394â†’                
   395â†’                htmlContent = result.join('\n');
   396â†’                
   397â†’                // Restore code blocks
   398â†’                codeBlocks.forEach((block, index) => {
   399â†’                    htmlContent = htmlContent.replace(`__CODE_BLOCK_${index}__`, block);
   400â†’                });
   401â†’                
   402â†’                // Clean up empty paragraphs and fix common issues
   403â†’                htmlContent = htmlContent
   404â†’                    .replace(/<p><\/p>/g, '')
   405â†’                    .replace(/<p>(<[^>]+>)/g, '$1')  // Remove p tags around block elements
   406â†’                    .replace(/(<\/[^>]+>)<\/p>/g, '$1');  // Remove closing p tags after block elements
   407â†’                
   408â†’                // Replace the content while preserving essential structure
   409â†’                contentArea.innerHTML = htmlContent;
   410â†’                
   411â†’                // Ensure content has proper MkDocs classes for scroll highlighting
   412â†’                if (!contentArea.classList.contains('md-typeset')) {
   413â†’                    contentArea.classList.add('md-typeset');
   414â†’                }
   415â†’                
   416â†’                // Fix navigation links within the injected content
   417â†’                this.fixNavigationLinks(contentArea);
   418â†’                
   419â†’                // Update page title based on content
   420â†’                this.updatePageTitle(markdownContent);
   421â†’                
   422â†’                // Update navigation state to match corporate content
   423â†’                const contentFile = this.getCurrentContentFile();
   424â†’                this.updateNavigationState(contentFile);
   425â†’                
   426â†’                console.log('âœ… Corporate content successfully injected with preserved structure');
   427â†’                
   428â†’            } catch (error) {
   429â†’                console.error('âŒ Failed to replace page content:', error);
   430â†’            } finally {
   431â†’                // Always reset the flag to allow future content replacements
   432â†’                this._isReplacingContent = false;
   433â†’            }
   434â†’        }
   435â†’
   436â†’        /**
   437â†’         * Triggers MkDocs navigation update for scroll highlighting
   438â†’         */
   439â†’        updateNavigationState(contentFile) {
   440â†’            try {
   441â†’                console.log('ğŸ”„ Updating navigation state for:', contentFile);
   442â†’                
   443â†’                // Update sidebar highlighting based on content
   444â†’                this.updateSidebarForContent(contentFile);
   445â†’                
   446â†’                // Simple scroll highlighting re-initialization without breaking MkDocs
   447â†’                setTimeout(() => {
   448â†’                    // Just trigger a scroll event to activate any existing highlighting
   449â†’                    window.dispatchEvent(new Event('scroll', { bubbles: true }));
   450â†’                }, 100);
   451â†’                
   452â†’                console.log('âœ… Navigation state updated');
   453â†’            } catch (error) {
   454â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Could not update navigation state:', error);
   455â†’            }
   456â†’        }
   457â†’
   458â†’        /**
   459â†’         * Updates sidebar highlighting based on corporate content
   460â†’         */
   461â†’        updateSidebarForContent(contentFile) {
   462â†’            try {
   463â†’                // First, ensure sidebar is visible (especially important for coder page)
   464â†’                this.ensureSidebarVisible();
   465â†’                
   466â†’                // Remove any existing active states
   467â†’                document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link--active, .md-nav__item--active').forEach(el => {
   468â†’                    el.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active', 'md-nav__item--active');
   469â†’                });
   470â†’                
   471â†’                // Determine which sidebar item should be highlighted
   472â†’                let targetText = '';
   473â†’                if (contentFile.includes('coder-detailed.md')) {
   474â†’                    targetText = 'Development Environment';
   475â†’                    // For the coder page, ensure we're in the correct navigation context
   476â†’                    this.ensureCoderPageNavigation();
   477â†’                } else if (contentFile.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md')) {
   478â†’                    targetText = 'Enterprise Integration';
   479â†’                }
   480â†’                
   481â†’                // Find and highlight the appropriate navigation item
   482â†’                if (targetText) {
   483â†’                    const navLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   484â†’                    navLinks.forEach(link => {
   485â†’                        if (link.textContent.includes(targetText)) {
   486â†’                            link.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   487â†’                            const item = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   488â†’                            if (item) {
   489â†’                                item.classList.add('md-nav__item--active');
   490â†’                            }
   491â†’                        }
   492â†’                    });
   493â†’                }
   494â†’                
   495â†’                console.log('âœ… Sidebar highlighting updated for:', targetText);
   496â†’            } catch (error) {
   497â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Could not update sidebar highlighting:', error);
   498â†’            }
   499â†’        }
   500â†’        
   501â†’        /**
   502â†’         * Ensures the sidebar is visible and properly displayed
   503â†’         */
   504â†’        ensureSidebarVisible() {
   505â†’            try {
   506â†’                // Log current sidebar state for debugging
   507â†’                const sidebar = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar.md-sidebar--primary');
   508â†’                if (sidebar) {
   509â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Current sidebar state:', {
   510â†’                        display: sidebar.style.display || 'default',
   511â†’                        visibility: sidebar.style.visibility || 'default',
   512â†’                        classes: sidebar.className,
   513â†’                        offsetWidth: sidebar.offsetWidth,
   514â†’                        offsetHeight: sidebar.offsetHeight
   515â†’                    });
   516â†’                    
   517â†’                    // Check screen size first
   518â†’                    const isNarrowScreen = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 76.1875em)').matches;
   519â†’                    const drawerToggle = document.querySelector('[data-md-toggle="drawer"]');
   520â†’                    
   521â†’                    if (isNarrowScreen) {
   522â†’                        // On narrow screens: drawer should be closed (checked = true)
   523â†’                        if (drawerToggle && drawerToggle.type === 'checkbox') {
   524â†’                            drawerToggle.checked = true; // Closed by default on mobile
   525â†’                            console.log('ğŸ“± Narrow screen - drawer closed');
   526â†’                        }
   527â†’                        // Clear any forced styles for mobile
   528â†’                        sidebar.style.removeProperty('display');
   529â†’                        sidebar.style.removeProperty('position');
   530â†’                        sidebar.style.removeProperty('left');
   531â†’                    } else {
   532â†’                        // On wide screens: sidebar should be visible (no !important overrides)
   533â†’                        sidebar.classList.remove('md-sidebar--hidden');
   534â†’                        
   535â†’                        // Use gentle CSS resets without !important
   536â†’                        sidebar.style.display = '';  // Use empty string to revert to CSS default
   537â†’                        sidebar.style.visibility = 'visible';
   538â†’                        sidebar.style.opacity = '1';
   539â†’                        
   540â†’                        if (drawerToggle && drawerToggle.type === 'checkbox') {
   541â†’                            drawerToggle.checked = false; // Unchecked = visible on desktop
   542â†’                            console.log('ğŸ–¥ï¸ Wide screen - sidebar visible');
   543â†’                        }
   544â†’                    }
   545â†’                    
   546â†’                    console.log('âœ… Sidebar responsive behavior restored');
   547â†’                } else {
   548â†’                    console.warn('âš ï¸ Primary sidebar not found in DOM');
   549â†’                }
   550â†’                
   551â†’                // Clear any forced styles on secondary sidebar (TOC) too
   552â†’                const secondarySidebar = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar.md-sidebar--secondary');
   553â†’                if (secondarySidebar) {
   554â†’                    secondarySidebar.style.removeProperty('display');
   555â†’                    secondarySidebar.style.removeProperty('visibility');
   556â†’                    secondarySidebar.style.removeProperty('opacity');
   557â†’                    secondarySidebar.style.removeProperty('position');
   558â†’                    console.log('âœ… Secondary sidebar responsive behavior restored');
   559â†’                }
   560â†’                
   561â†’                // Try to reinitialize Material theme if possible
   562â†’                setTimeout(() => {
   563â†’                    try {
   564â†’                        if (window.app && window.app.drawer) {
   565â†’                            window.app.drawer.reset();
   566â†’                        }
   567â†’                        // Force body class update to ensure proper layout
   568â†’                        document.body.classList.remove('md-sidebar--hidden');
   569â†’                        document.documentElement.classList.remove('md-sidebar--hidden');
   570â†’                    } catch (e) {
   571â†’                        console.log('Could not reinitialize Material theme:', e);
   572â†’                    }
   573â†’                }, 100);
   574â†’                
   575â†’            } catch (error) {
   576â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Could not ensure sidebar visibility:', error);
   577â†’            }
   578â†’        }
   579â†’        
   580â†’        /**
   581â†’         * Ensures proper navigation context for the coder page
   582â†’         */
   583â†’        ensureCoderPageNavigation() {
   584â†’            try {
   585â†’                // Find the "Setup & Environment" section in navigation
   586â†’                const setupSection = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link')).find(link =>
   587â†’                    link.textContent.includes('Setup & Environment') || 
   588â†’                    link.textContent.includes('Getting Started')
   589â†’                );
   590â†’                
   591â†’                if (setupSection) {
   592â†’                    // Expand the parent section if needed
   593â†’                    const parentItem = setupSection.closest('.md-nav__item');
   594â†’                    if (parentItem) {
   595â†’                        const toggle = parentItem.querySelector('[data-md-toggle]');
   596â†’                        if (toggle && toggle.type === 'checkbox') {
   597â†’                            toggle.checked = true; // Expand the section
   598â†’                        }
   599â†’                    }
   600â†’                }
   601â†’                
   602â†’                console.log('âœ… Coder page navigation context set');
   603â†’            } catch (error) {
   604â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Could not set coder page navigation:', error);
   605â†’            }
   606â†’        }

   613â†’        /**
   614â†’         * Gets the current content file being displayed
   615â†’         */
   616â†’        getCurrentContentFile() {
   617â†’            const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
   618â†’            
   619â†’            if (currentPath.includes('/00_intro/coder/')) {
   620â†’                return '00_intro/coder-detailed.md';
   621â†’            } else if (currentPath.includes('/00_intro/llmapi/')) {
   622â†’                return '00_intro/llmapi-detailed.md';
   623â†’            } else if (currentPath.includes('/03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment/')) {
   624â†’                return '03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md';
   625â†’            }
   626â†’            
   627â†’            return null;
   628â†’        }

   630â†’        /**
   631â†’         * Updates page title and header based on content
   632â†’         */
   633â†’        updatePageTitle(content) {
   634â†’            try {
   635â†’                // Extract first H1 heading from content for dynamic title
   636â†’                const h1Match = content.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m);
   637â†’                if (h1Match) {
   638â†’                    const pageTitle = h1Match[1].trim();
   639â†’                    document.title = `${pageTitle} - Agentic AI Nano-Degree`;
   640â†’                    
   641â†’                    // Update header title if available
   642â†’                    const headerTopic = document.querySelector('.md-header__topic[data-md-component="header-topic"] .md-ellipsis');
   643â†’                    if (headerTopic) {
   644â†’                        headerTopic.textContent = pageTitle;
   645â†’                    }
   646â†’                    
   647â†’                    console.log('âœ… Page title updated:', pageTitle);
   648â†’                }
   649â†’            } catch (error) {
   650â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Could not update page title:', error);
   651â†’            }
   652â†’        }
   653â†’
   654â†’
   655â†’        /**
   656â†’         * Replaces image references in markdown with base64 data URLs from encrypted content
   657â†’         */
   658â†’        async replaceImagesWithBase64(markdownContent) {
   659â†’            let processedContent = markdownContent;
   660â†’            
   661â†’            // Find all image references in markdown: ![alt](path)
   662â†’            const imagePattern = /!\[([^\]]*)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g;
   663â†’            const matches = [...markdownContent.matchAll(imagePattern)];
   664â†’            
   665â†’            for (const match of matches) {
   666â†’                const [fullMatch, altText, imagePath] = match;
   667â†’                console.log(`ğŸ–¼ï¸ Processing image: ${imagePath}`);
   668â†’                
   669â†’                // Normalize the image path to match encrypted content keys
   670â†’                let normalizedPath = this.normalizeImagePath(imagePath);
   671â†’                
   672â†’                // Look for the image in encrypted content
   673â†’                if (this.loadedContent[normalizedPath]) {
   674â†’                    const base64Content = this.loadedContent[normalizedPath];
   675â†’                    const extension = normalizedPath.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
   676â†’                    const mimeType = this.getMimeType(extension);
   677â†’                    const dataUrl = `data:${mimeType};base64,${base64Content}`;
   678â†’                    
   679â†’                    // Replace the image reference with base64 data URL
   680â†’                    processedContent = processedContent.replace(fullMatch, `![${altText}](${dataUrl})`);
   681â†’                    console.log(`âœ… Replaced image ${normalizedPath} with base64 data URL`);
   682â†’                } else {
   683â†’                    // If not in encrypted content, it might be a shared image
   684â†’                    // Keep the original path but adjust for correct web path
   685â†’                    if (imagePath.includes('../../00_intro/images/')) {
   686â†’                        // Shared images - adjust path for web access
   687â†’                        const webPath = imagePath.replace('../../', '/agentic-ai-nano/');
   688â†’                        processedContent = processedContent.replace(fullMatch, `![${altText}](${webPath})`);
   689â†’                        console.log(`ğŸ“· Using shared image with web path: ${webPath}`);
   690â†’                    } else {
   691â†’                        console.warn(`âŒ Image not found in encrypted content: ${normalizedPath}`);
   692â†’                        console.log('Available encrypted images:', Object.keys(this.loadedContent).filter(key => key.match(/\.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg)$/i)));
   693â†’                    }
   694â†’                }
   695â†’            }
   696â†’            
   697â†’            return processedContent;
   698â†’        }
   699â†’
   700â†’        /**
   701â†’         * Normalizes image paths to match encrypted content structure
   702â†’         */
   703â†’        normalizeImagePath(imagePath) {
   704â†’            // Remove leading ../ or ./ and normalize path separators
   705â†’            let normalized = imagePath.replace(/\\/g, '/');
   706â†’            
   707â†’            // Handle different path patterns in corporate content
   708â†’            if (imagePath.includes('../../corporate-only/')) {
   709â†’                // Path like ../../corporate-only/images/file.png -> images/file.png
   710â†’                normalized = imagePath.replace('../../corporate-only/', '');
   711â†’            } else if (imagePath.startsWith('../images/')) {
   712â†’                // Path like ../images/file.png -> images/file.png (corporate-only images)
   713â†’                normalized = imagePath.replace('../images/', 'images/');
   714â†’            } else if (imagePath.includes('../../00_intro/images/')) {
   715â†’                // Path like ../../00_intro/images/file.png -> 00_intro/images/file.png (shared images)
   716â†’                normalized = imagePath.replace('../../', '');
   717â†’            } else if (imagePath.startsWith('images/')) {
   718â†’                // Already normalized
   719â†’                normalized = imagePath;
   720â†’            }
   721â†’            
   722â†’            console.log(`ğŸ“ Normalized image path: ${imagePath} -> ${normalized}`);
   723â†’            return normalized;
   724â†’        }
   725â†’
   726â†’        /**
   727â†’         * Injects decrypted markdown content (legacy method, kept for compatibility)
   728â†’         */
   729â†’        async injectMarkdownContent(filePath, content) {
   730â†’            // Look for elements that reference this file path
   731â†’            const selector = `[href*="${filePath}"], [src*="${filePath}"]`;
   732â†’            const elements = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
   733â†’            
   734â†’            if (elements.length > 0) {
   735â†’                console.log(`ğŸ’‰ Injecting markdown content for ${filePath}`);
   736â†’                // Convert markdown to HTML and inject
   737â†’                // This would require a markdown parser or server-side rendering
   738â†’                // For now, just log that content is available
   739â†’                console.log(`ğŸ“„ Content available for ${filePath} (${content.length} chars)`);
   740â†’            }
   741â†’        }
   742â†’
   743â†’        /**
   744â†’         * Injects decrypted image content
   745â†’         */

   747â†’            // Find img elements with src pointing to this file

   261â†’        // Update network status indicator
   262â†’        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('corporate');
   263â†’    }
   264â†’
   265â†’    function hideCorporateContent() {
   266â†’        console.log('ğŸŒ Showing public content');

   288â†’        removeSession10Navigation();

   294â†’        updateNetworkSpecificContent(false);
   295â†’        
   296â†’        // Update network status indicator
   297â†’        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('public');
   298â†’    }

   330â†’    function updateNetworkStatusIndicator(networkType) {
   331â†’        // Only show indicator on Setup & Environment pages
   332â†’        const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
   333â†’        const isSetupPage = currentPath.includes('00_intro') || 
   334â†’                           currentPath.includes('setup') || 
   335â†’                           currentPath.includes('environment') ||
   336â†’                           currentPath.includes('coder') ||
   337â†’                           currentPath.includes('llmapi');
   338â†’        
   339â†’        // Remove any existing status indicator
   340â†’        const existingIndicator = document.querySelector('.network-status-indicator');
   341â†’        if (existingIndicator) {
   342â†’            existingIndicator.remove();
   343â†’        }
   344â†’
   345â†’        // Don't show indicator if not on setup pages
   346â†’        if (!isSetupPage) {
   347â†’            return;
   348â†’        }
   349â†’
   350â†’        // Create new status indicator
   351â†’        const indicator = document.createElement('div');
   352â†’        indicator.className = 'network-status-indicator';
   353â†’        indicator.style.cssText = `
   354â†’            position: fixed;
   355â†’            bottom: 20px;
   356â†’            right: 20px;
   357â†’            background: ${networkType === 'corporate' ? '#0066cc' : '#28a745'};
   358â†’            color: white;
   359â†’            padding: 8px 12px;
   360â†’            border-radius: 4px;
   361â†’            font-size: 12px;
   362â†’            font-weight: bold;
   363â†’            z-index: 1000;
   364â†’            box-shadow: 0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);
   365â†’            font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif;
   366â†’        `;
   367â†’        
   368â†’        if (networkType === 'corporate') {
   369â†’            indicator.innerHTML = `
   370â†’                ğŸ¢ BMW Corporate Network
   371â†’                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   372â†’                    Cloud Dev Environment Available
   373â†’                </div>
   374â†’            `;
   375â†’        } else if (networkType === 'checking') {
   376â†’            indicator.innerHTML = `
   377â†’                ğŸ” Detecting Network...
   378â†’                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   379â†’                    Checking corporate access
   380â†’                </div>
   381â†’            `;
   382â†’            indicator.style.background = '#ffa500';
   383â†’        } else {
   384â†’            indicator.innerHTML = `
   385â†’                ğŸŒ Public Network
   386â†’                <div style="font-size: 10px; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 2px;">
   387â†’                    Local Setup Required
   388â†’                </div>
   389â†’            `;
   390â†’        }
   391â†’
   392â†’        // Remove manual override clickability to prevent switching to corporate network
   393â†’        // This was causing unwanted CN switching when viewing publicly
   394â†’        indicator.style.cursor = 'default';
   395â†’        indicator.title = networkType === 'corporate' ? 
   396â†’            'BMW Corporate Network - Cloud Development Environment Available' : 
   397â†’            'Public Network - Local Setup Required';
   398â†’
   399â†’        document.body.appendChild(indicator);
   400â†’
   401â†’        // Auto-hide after 5 seconds
   402â†’        setTimeout(() => {
   403â†’            if (indicator && indicator.parentNode) {
   404â†’                indicator.style.transition = 'opacity 0.5s ease';
   405â†’                indicator.style.opacity = '0';
   406â†’                setTimeout(() => {
   407â†’                    if (indicator && indicator.parentNode) {
   408â†’                        indicator.remove();
   409â†’                    }
   410â†’                }, 500);
   411â†’            }
   412â†’        }, 5000);
   413â†’    }
   414â†’
   415â†’    function initializeNetworkDetection() {
   416â†’        // Add CSS for smooth transitions and ensure BMW content is hidden by default on public sites
   417â†’        const style = document.createElement('style');
   418â†’        const hostname = window.location.hostname;
   419â†’        const isPublicSite = hostname.includes('github.io') || hostname.includes('fwornle');
   420â†’        
   421â†’        style.textContent = `
   422â†’            /* Default: hide all conditional content until detection completes */
   423â†’            .bmw-corporate-only {
   424â†’                display: none;
   425â†’                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   426â†’            }
   427â†’            .bmw-public-alternative {
   428â†’                display: none;
   429â†’                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   430â†’            }
   431â†’            /* Show corporate content when detected */
   432â†’            .bmw-corporate-only.corporate-network-detected {
   433â†’                display: block;
   434â†’                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   435â†’            }
   436â†’            /* Show public content when detected */
   437â†’            .bmw-public-alternative.public-network-detected {
   438â†’                display: block;
   439â†’                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   440â†’            }
   441â†’            @keyframes fadeIn {
   442â†’                from { opacity: 0; }
   443â†’                to { opacity: 1; }
   444â†’            }
   445â†’            /* Ensure setup instructions container is visible */
   446â†’            .setup-instructions {
   447â†’                min-height: 100px;
   448â†’            }
   449â†’        `;
   450â†’        document.head.appendChild(style);
   451â†’
   452â†’        // Always run CN detection regardless of hostname
   453â†’        console.log('Running corporate network detection...');
   454â†’        
   455â†’        // Initial quick check, then run full detection
   456â†’        if (isCorporateNetwork()) {
   457â†’            console.log('Corporate network detected initially');
   458â†’            showCorporateContent();
   459â†’        } else {
   460â†’            console.log('Public network assumed initially, running full CN detection');
   461â†’            hideCorporateContent();
   462â†’            // Always run the comprehensive check for CN access
   463â†’            checkInternalService();
   464â†’        }
   465â†’    }
   466â†’
   467â†’    function cleanupNavigationState() {
   468â†’        // Clean up any previous navigation state
   469â†’        // We're on a corporate page, so just reset for fresh setup
   470â†’        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
   471â†’            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
   472â†’            window.corporateScrollListener = null;
   473â†’            console.log('ğŸ§¹ Cleaned up previous corporate scroll listener');
   474â†’        }
   475â†’    }
   476â†’
   477â†’    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load
   478â†’    function runDetection() {
   479â†’        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections
   480â†’        if (detectionInProgress) {
   481â†’            console.log('ğŸ”„ Detection already in progress, skipping...');
   482â†’            return;
   483â†’        }
   484â†’        
   485â†’        // Clear any pending detection
   486â†’        if (detectionTimeout) {
   487â†’            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);
   488â†’        }
   489â†’        
   490â†’        // Debounce detection to prevent rapid successive calls
   491â†’        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   492â†’            if (detectionInProgress) return;
   493â†’            
   494â†’            detectionInProgress = true;
   495â†’            console.log('ğŸ”„ Starting fresh network detection...');
   496â†’            
   497â†’            // Clean up navigation state first
   498â†’            cleanupNavigationState();
   499â†’            
   500â†’            try {
   501â†’                initializeNetworkDetection();
   502â†’            } finally {
   503â†’                // Reset detection flag after a delay to allow for async operations
   504â†’                setTimeout(() => {
   505â†’                    detectionInProgress = false;
   506â†’                }, 2000);
   507â†’            }
   508â†’        }, 100);
   509â†’    }
   510â†’    
   511â†’    // Initial run
   512â†’    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
   513â†’        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', runDetection);
   514â†’    } else {
   515â†’        runDetection();
   516â†’    }
   517â†’    
   518â†’    // Set up navigation listeners immediately (not waiting for DOMContentLoaded)
   519â†’    console.log('ğŸ¯ Setting up navigation listeners');
   520â†’    
   521â†’    // Watch for URL changes with MutationObserver
   522â†’    let lastUrl = location.href;
   523â†’    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
   524â†’        const url = location.href;
   525â†’        if (url !== lastUrl) {
   526â†’            lastUrl = url;
   527â†’            console.log('ğŸ“ URL changed to:', url);
   528â†’            
   529â†’            // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating to different pages
   530â†’            if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   531â†’                session10Loaded = false;
   532â†’            }
   533â†’            
   534â†’            // No cleanup needed - if we navigate away, the page will reload
   535â†’            // and our early exit will prevent this code from running
   536â†’            
   537â†’            setTimeout(runDetection, 100);
   538â†’        }
   539â†’    });
   540â†’    observer.observe(document.body || document.documentElement, {
   541â†’        subtree: true, 
   542â†’        childList: true
   543â†’    });
   544â†’    
   545â†’    // Listen for navigation link clicks (use capturing to catch all clicks)
   546â†’    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   547â†’        const link = e.target.closest('a');
   548â†’        if (link) {
   549â†’            const href = link.getAttribute('href');
   550â†’            console.log('ğŸ”— Link clicked:', href);
   551â†’            if (link.classList.contains('md-nav__link') || 
   552â†’                link.classList.contains('md-tabs__link') ||
   553â†’                href?.includes('/00_intro/')) {
   554â†’                console.log('ğŸ”— Navigation link detected, will re-run detection');
   555â†’                setTimeout(runDetection, 500);
   556â†’            }
   557â†’        }
   558â†’    }, true); // Use capture phase
   559â†’    
   560â†’    // Also listen for popstate
   561â†’    window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
   562â†’        console.log('â¬…ï¸ Browser navigation detected');
   563â†’        
   564â†’        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating back/forward
   565â†’        const url = location.href;
   566â†’        if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   567â†’            session10Loaded = false;
   568â†’        }
   569â†’        
   570â†’        runDetection();
   571â†’    });
   572â†’

   576â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   577â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   578â†’            // Hide items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   579â†’            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   580â†’                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   581â†’                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   582â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   583â†’                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   584â†’                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   585â†’                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   586â†’                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   587â†’                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   588â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   589â†’                if (listItem) {
   590â†’                    console.log('Hiding corporate nav item:', linkText);
   591â†’                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
   592â†’                }
   593â†’            }
   594â†’        });
   595â†’    }
   596â†’
   597â†’    function showCorporateNavigationItems() {
   598â†’        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   599â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {

   601â†’            // Show items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators

   603â†’                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   604â†’                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   605â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   606â†’                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   607â†’                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   608â†’                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   609â†’                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   610â†’                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   611â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   612â†’                if (listItem) {
   613â†’                    console.log('Showing corporate nav item:', linkText);

   622â†’
   623â†’    function addSession10Navigation() {
   624â†’        // Find Session 9 in Module 03 navigation and add Session 10 after it
   625â†’        const session9Link = document.querySelector('a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]');
   626â†’        if (session9Link) {
   627â†’            const session9Item = session9Link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   628â†’            if (session9Item && !document.querySelector('.bmw-corporate-nav-item')) {
   629â†’                console.log('ğŸ”§ Adding Session 10 to corporate navigation');
   630â†’                
   631â†’                // Create Session 10 navigation item
   632â†’                const session10Item = document.createElement('li');
   633â†’                session10Item.className = 'md-nav__item bmw-corporate-nav-item';
   634â†’                
   635â†’                const session10Link = document.createElement('a');
   636â†’                session10Link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   637â†’                session10Link.className = 'md-nav__link bmw-corporate-link';
   638â†’                session10Link.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   639â†’                
   640â†’                // Add click handler to load corporate content
   641â†’                session10Link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   642â†’                    e.preventDefault();
   643â†’                    loadCorporateSession10();
   644â†’                });
   645â†’                
   646â†’                session10Item.appendChild(session10Link);
   647â†’                
   648â†’                // Insert after Session 9
   649â†’                session9Item.parentNode.insertBefore(session10Item, session9Item.nextSibling);
   650â†’                
   651â†’                console.log('âœ… Session 10 added to corporate navigation');
   652â†’            }
   653â†’        }
   654â†’        
   655â†’        // Also update the "Next" link on Session 9 to point to Session 10
   656â†’        updateSession9NextLink();
   657â†’    }
   658â†’
   659â†’    function updateSession9NextLink() {
   660â†’        // Find "Next" navigation links and update Session 9 to point to Session 10
   661â†’        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
   662â†’        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
   663â†’            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {
   664â†’                const titleDiv = link.querySelector('.md-ellipsis');
   665â†’                if (titleDiv) {
   666â†’                    titleDiv.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   667â†’                    link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   668â†’                    
   669â†’                    // Add click handler for corporate Session 10
   670â†’                    link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   671â†’                        e.preventDefault();
   672â†’                        loadCorporateSession10();
   673â†’                    });
   674â†’                    
   675â†’                    console.log('ğŸ”§ Updated Session 9 next link to point to Session 10');
   676â†’                }
   677â†’            }
   678â†’        });
   679â†’    }
   680â†’
   681â†’    // Track if Session 10 content is currently loaded to prevent multiple loads
   682â†’    let session10Loaded = false;
   683â†’    
   684â†’    window.loadCorporateSession10 = async function() {
   685â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Loading corporate Session 10 content...');
   686â†’        
   687â†’        // Prevent multiple loads of Session 10 content
   688â†’        if (session10Loaded) {
   689â†’            console.log('ğŸ“„ Session 10 already loaded, skipping...');
   690â†’            return true;
   691â†’        }
   692â†’        
   693â†’        // Retry mechanism for improved reliability
   694â†’        const maxRetries = 3;
   695â†’        let retryCount = 0;
   696â†’        
   697â†’        while (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   698â†’            try {
   699â†’                console.log(`ğŸ”„ Attempt ${retryCount + 1}/${maxRetries} to load Session 10...`);
   700â†’                
   701â†’                // Check if corporate content loader exists
   702â†’                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader) {
   703â†’                    console.warn('âš ï¸ Corporate content loader not available, waiting...');
   704â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   705â†’                    retryCount++;
   706â†’                    continue;
   707â†’                }
   708â†’                
   709â†’                // If content is not loaded yet, try to load it first
   710â†’                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent) {
   711â†’                    console.log('ğŸ“¥ Corporate content not loaded yet, loading now...');
   712â†’                    const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
   713â†’                    if (!loaded) {
   714â†’                        console.warn('âš ï¸ Failed to load corporate content, retrying...');
   715â†’                        retryCount++;
   716â†’                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   717â†’                        continue;
   718â†’                    }
   719â†’                    console.log('âœ… Corporate content loaded successfully');
   720â†’                }
   721â†’                
   722â†’                // Now check for Session 10 content
   723â†’                const session10Content = window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent['03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md'];
   724â†’                if (session10Content) {
   725â†’                    console.log('ğŸ“„ Found Session 10 content, replacing page...');
   726â†’                    session10Loaded = true;
   727â†’                    
   728â†’                    // Update page title
   729â†’                    document.title = 'Session 10: Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment | Agentic AI Nano-Degree';
   730â†’                    
   731â†’                    // Update URL without causing page reload - use hash instead of path to avoid 404s
   732â†’                    if (history.pushState) {
   733â†’                        // Use hash-based navigation to avoid creating non-existent paths
   734â†’                        const baseUrl = window.location.pathname.replace(/#.*$/, '');
   735â†’                        const newUrl = baseUrl + '#session10-corporate-content';
   736â†’                        history.pushState({page: 'session10'}, '', newUrl);
   737â†’                    }
   738â†’                    
   739â†’                    // Replace page content
   740â†’                    await window.CorporateContentLoader.replacePageContent(session10Content);
   741â†’                    
   742â†’                    // Wait a bit for content to be injected, then update navigation
   743â†’                    setTimeout(async () => {
   744â†’                        await updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(session10Content);
   745â†’                    }, 100);
   746â†’                    
   747â†’                    // Instantly jump to top of the page after content is loaded
   748â†’                    setTimeout(() => {
   749â†’                        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
   750â†’                        console.log('ğŸ“ Jumped to top of Session 10 content');
   751â†’                    }, 200);
   752â†’                    
   753â†’                    console.log('âœ… Session 10 corporate content loaded successfully');
   754â†’                    return true;
   755â†’                    
   756â†’                } else {
   757â†’                    console.warn('âš ï¸ Session 10 content not found in encrypted data, retrying...');
   758â†’                    console.log('Available content keys:', Object.keys(window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent || {}));
   759â†’                    retryCount++;
   760â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   761â†’                    continue;
   762â†’                }
   763â†’                
   764â†’            } catch (error) {
   765â†’                console.warn(`âš ï¸ Error loading Session 10 (attempt ${retryCount + 1}):`, error);
   766â†’                retryCount++;
   767â†’                if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   768â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   769â†’                }
   770â†’            }
   771â†’        }
   772â†’        
   773â†’        console.error('âŒ Failed to load Session 10 after all retries');
   774â†’        return false;
   775â†’    }
   776â†’
   777â†’    async function updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(contentMarkdown) {
   778â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Updating MkDocs navigation for corporate content...');
   779â†’        
   780â†’        // No guard needed - we're already on a corporate content page if this runs
   781â†’        
   782â†’        try {
   783â†’            // Extract metadata from the content itself
   784â†’            const contentMetadata = extractContentMetadata(contentMarkdown);
   785â†’            console.log('ğŸ“„ Detected content metadata:', contentMetadata);
   786â†’            
   787â†’            // Wait for MkDocs navigation to be ready (retry mechanism)
   788â†’            let attempts = 0;
   789â†’            const maxAttempts = 5;
   790â†’            let corporateNavItem = null;
   791â†’            
   792â†’            while (!corporateNavItem && attempts < maxAttempts) {
   793â†’                if (attempts > 0) {
   794â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200 * attempts)); // Progressive delay
   795â†’                }
   796â†’                
   797â†’                // Debug: List all navigation links on first attempt
   798â†’                if (attempts === 0) {
   799â†’                    const allNavLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   800â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Debug - All navigation links found:', allNavLinks.length);
   801â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Navigation structure:', Array.from(allNavLinks).slice(0, 10).map(link => ({
   802â†’                        href: link.getAttribute('href'),
   803â†’                        text: link.textContent.trim(),
   804â†’                        active: link.classList.contains('md-nav__link--active')
   805â†’                    })));
   806â†’                }
   807â†’                
   808â†’                // First try to find current active navigation item
   809â†’                corporateNavItem = document.querySelector('.md-nav__link--active')?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   810â†’                
   811â†’                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   812â†’                    // Try specific Session 9 patterns
   813â†’                    const session9Selectors = [
   814â†’                        'a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]',
   815â†’                        'a[href*="Session9"]',
   816â†’                        'a[href*="Production_Agent_Deployment"]'
   817â†’                    ];
   818â†’                    
   819â†’                    for (const selector of session9Selectors) {
   820â†’                        corporateNavItem = document.querySelector(selector)?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   821â†’                        if (corporateNavItem) {
   822â†’                            console.log(`ğŸ¯ Found via selector: ${selector}`);
   823â†’                            break;
   824â†’                        }
   825â†’                    }
   826â†’                }
   827â†’                
   828â†’                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   829â†’                    // Fallback: try any MCP/ACP section navigation item
   830â†’                    corporateNavItem = document.querySelector([
   831â†’                        'a[href*="03_mcp-acp-a2a"]',
   832â†’                        'a[href*="mcp-acp-a2a"]'
   833â†’                    ].join(', '))?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   834â†’                }
   835â†’                
   836â†’                attempts++;
   837â†’                console.log(`ğŸ” Navigation search attempt ${attempts}/${maxAttempts}, found:`, !!corporateNavItem);
   838â†’                
   839â†’                if (corporateNavItem) {
   840â†’                    const navLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   841â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Found navigation item:', {
   842â†’                        href: navLink?.getAttribute('href'),
   843â†’                        text: navLink?.textContent?.trim(),
   844â†’                        outerHTML: corporateNavItem.outerHTML.substring(0, 200) + '...'
   845â†’                    });
   846â†’                }
   847â†’            }
   848â†’            
   849â†’            if (corporateNavItem) {
   850â†’                // Remove active state from all navigation items
   851â†’                document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__item').forEach(item => {
   852â†’                    item.classList.remove('md-nav__item--active');
   853â†’                    const link = item.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   854â†’                    if (link) {
   855â†’                        link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
   856â†’                    }
   857â†’                });
   858â†’                
   859â†’                // Activate corporate content navigation item
   860â†’                corporateNavItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--active');
   861â†’                const corporateLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   862â†’                if (corporateLink) {
   863â†’                    corporateLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   864â†’                    // Update the link text to match current content
   865â†’                    if (contentMetadata.title) {
   866â†’                        corporateLink.textContent = contentMetadata.title;
   867â†’                    }
   868â†’                }
   869â†’                
   870â†’                // Create corporate content sub-navigation based on content structure
   871â†’                createCorporateContentSubNavigation(corporateNavItem, contentMetadata);
   872â†’                
   873â†’                // Scroll corporate content item into view in sidebar
   874â†’                corporateNavItem.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
   875â†’                
   876â†’                console.log(`âœ… MkDocs navigation updated for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}`);
   877â†’            } else {
   878â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Corporate content navigation item not found');
   879â†’            }
   880â†’            
   881â†’            // Fix potential sidebar styling conflicts
   882â†’            fixSidebarStylingConflicts();
   883â†’            
   884â†’        } catch (error) {
   885â†’            console.error('âŒ Failed to update MkDocs navigation for corporate content:', error);
   886â†’        }
   887â†’    }
   888â†’
   889â†’    function extractContentMetadata(markdownContent) {
   890â†’        const metadata = {
   891â†’            title: null,
   892â†’            sections: [],
   893â†’            type: 'corporate-content'
   894â†’        };
   895â†’        
   896â†’        if (!markdownContent) return metadata;
   897â†’        
   898â†’        // Extract title from first H1
   899â†’        const titleMatch = markdownContent.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m);
   900â†’        if (titleMatch) {
   901â†’            metadata.title = titleMatch[1].trim();
   902â†’        }
   903â†’        
   904â†’        // Extract sections from H2 and H3 headings
   905â†’        const headingMatches = markdownContent.match(/^#{2,3}\s+(.+)$/gm);
   906â†’        if (headingMatches) {
   907â†’            metadata.sections = headingMatches.map(heading => {
   908â†’                const level = (heading.match(/#/g) || []).length;
   909â†’                const title = heading.replace(/^#+\s+/, '').trim();
   910â†’                const id = title.toLowerCase()
   911â†’                    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
   912â†’                    .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
   913â†’                    .replace(/-+/g, '-')
   914â†’                    .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
   915â†’                
   916â†’                return {
   917â†’                    level,
   918â†’                    title,
   919â†’                    id: id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-'),
   920â†’                    href: `#${id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`
   921â†’                };
   922â†’            });
   923â†’        }
   924â†’        
   925â†’        // Detect content type from title or content
   926â†’        if (metadata.title) {
   927â†’            if (metadata.title.includes('Session')) {
   928â†’                metadata.type = 'session';
   929â†’                // Extract session number if present
   930â†’                const sessionMatch = metadata.title.match(/Session\s*(\d+)/i);
   931â†’                if (sessionMatch) {
   932â†’                    metadata.sessionNumber = parseInt(sessionMatch[1]);
   933â†’                }
   934â†’            } else if (metadata.title.includes('Enterprise') || metadata.title.includes('Production')) {
   935â†’                metadata.type = 'enterprise-content';
   936â†’            }
   937â†’        }
   938â†’        
   939â†’        return metadata;
   940â†’    }
   941â†’
   942â†’
   943â†’    function createCorporateContentSubNavigation(navItem, contentMetadata) {
   944â†’        console.log(`ğŸ”§ Creating sub-navigation for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}...`);
   945â†’        
   946â†’        // Remove any existing sub-navigation to rebuild with current content
   947â†’        const existingSubNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
   948â†’        if (existingSubNav) {
   949â†’            existingSubNav.remove();
   950â†’        }
   951â†’        
   952â†’        // Debug content metadata
   953â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Content metadata for sub-navigation:', contentMetadata);
   954â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Available sections:', contentMetadata.sections);
   955â†’        
   956â†’        // Only create sub-navigation if we have sections
   957â†’        if (contentMetadata.sections && contentMetadata.sections.length > 0) {
   958â†’            // Create sub-navigation structure
   959â†’            const subNav = document.createElement('nav');
   960â†’            subNav.className = 'md-nav md-nav--secondary';
   961â†’            subNav.setAttribute('aria-label', `${contentMetadata.title || 'Corporate Content'} Navigation`);
   962â†’            
   963â†’            const subNavList = document.createElement('ul');
   964â†’            subNavList.className = 'md-nav__list';
   965â†’            
   966â†’            // Create navigation items from content sections
   967â†’            contentMetadata.sections.forEach(section => {
   968â†’                const listItem = document.createElement('li');
   969â†’                listItem.className = 'md-nav__item';
   970â†’                
   971â†’                const link = document.createElement('a');
   972â†’                link.href = section.href;
   973â†’                link.className = 'md-nav__link';
   974â†’                link.textContent = section.title;
   975â†’                
   976â†’                // Add appropriate nesting class for H3 items
   977â†’                if (section.level === 3) {
   978â†’                    listItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested');
   979â†’                }
   980â†’                
   981â†’                // Add smooth scroll behavior for anchor links
   982â†’                link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   983â†’                    e.preventDefault();
   984â†’                    const targetId = section.id;
   985â†’                    const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId) || 
   986â†’                                         document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${targetId}"]`) ||
   987â†’                                         findHeadingByText(section.title);
   988â†’                    
   989â†’                    if (targetElement) {
   990â†’                        targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
   991â†’                        // Update URL hash
   992â†’                        history.pushState(null, '', section.href);
   993â†’                        
   994â†’                        // Update active state in sub-navigation
   995â†’                        subNavList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(l => l.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active'));
   996â†’                        link.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   997â†’                    }
   998â†’                });
   999â†’                
  1000â†’                listItem.appendChild(link);
  1001â†’                subNavList.appendChild(listItem);
  1002â†’            });
  1003â†’            
  1004â†’            subNav.appendChild(subNavList);
  1005â†’            navItem.appendChild(subNav);
  1006â†’            
  1007â†’            console.log(`âœ… Sub-navigation created with ${contentMetadata.sections.length} sections`);
  1008â†’            
  1009â†’            // Set up scroll spy for corporate content - we're already on a corporate page
  1010â†’            setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(subNavList, contentMetadata.sections);
  1011â†’        }
  1012â†’        
  1013â†’        // Mark as corporate content for scroll spy detection
  1014â†’        document.body.classList.add('corporate-content-active');
  1015â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Marked page as corporate content');
  1016â†’        
  1017â†’        // Expand the navigation and ensure visibility
  1018â†’        navItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested', 'md-nav__item--active', 'corporate-nav-item');
  1019â†’        
  1020â†’        // Make sure the navigation item is visible and expanded
  1021â†’        const navInput = navItem.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
  1022â†’        if (navInput) {
  1023â†’            navInput.checked = true;
  1024â†’        }
  1025â†’        
  1026â†’        // Add explicit CSS to ensure visibility and prevent removal
  1027â†’        navItem.style.display = 'block !important';
  1028â†’        navItem.setAttribute('data-corporate-nav', 'true');
  1029â†’        const subNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
  1030â†’        if (subNav) {
  1031â†’            subNav.style.display = 'block !important';
  1032â†’            subNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1033â†’            subNav.setAttribute('data-corporate-subnav', 'true');
  1034â†’        }
  1035â†’        
  1036â†’        // Prevent navigation from being hidden by other scripts
  1037â†’        const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
  1038â†’            mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
  1039â†’                if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
  1040â†’                    const target = mutation.target;
  1041â†’                    if (target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-nav') || target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-subnav')) {
  1042â†’                        if (target.style.display === 'none' || target.style.visibility === 'hidden') {
  1043â†’                            console.log('ğŸ”§ Preventing corporate navigation from being hidden');
  1044â†’                            target.style.display = 'block';
  1045â†’                            target.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1046â†’                        }
  1047â†’                    }
  1048â†’                }
  1049â†’            });
  1050â†’        });
  1051â†’        
  1052â†’        observer.observe(navItem, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1053â†’        if (subNav) {
  1054â†’            observer.observe(subNav, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1055â†’        }
  1056â†’        
  1057â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Navigation item expanded and protected from hiding');
  1058â†’    }
  1059â†’
  1060â†’    function findHeadingByText(text) {
  1061â†’        // Helper function to find headings by text content
  1062â†’        const headings = document.querySelectorAll('h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6');
  1063â†’        for (const heading of headings) {
  1064â†’            if (heading.textContent.trim().toLowerCase().includes(text.toLowerCase())) {
  1065â†’                return heading;
  1066â†’            }
  1067â†’        }
  1068â†’        return null;
  1069â†’    }
  1070â†’
  1071â†’    function setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(navList, sections) {
  1072â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Setting up scroll spy for corporate content navigation...');
  1073â†’        
  1074â†’        let ticking = false;
  1075â†’        let lastActiveSection = null;
  1076â†’        let scrollSpyActive = false;
  1077â†’        
  1078â†’        function updateActiveNavigation() {
  1079â†’            if (!navList || !sections) return;
  1080â†’            
  1081â†’            // Find which section is currently visible
  1082â†’            let activeSection = null;
  1083â†’            const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  1084â†’            
  1085â†’            // Check each section to find the currently visible one
  1086â†’            for (let i = sections.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  1087â†’                const section = sections[i];
  1088â†’                const targetElement = document.getElementById(section.id) || 
  1089â†’                                   document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${section.id}"]`) ||
  1090â†’                                   findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1091â†’                
  1092â†’                if (targetElement) {
  1093â†’                    const rect = targetElement.getBoundingClientRect();
  1094â†’                    const elementTop = rect.top + scrollTop;
  1095â†’                    
  1096â†’                    // Consider element active if it's within the viewport or just passed
  1097â†’                    if (elementTop <= scrollTop + 100) {
  1098â†’                        activeSection = section;
  1099â†’                        break;
  1100â†’                    }
  1101â†’                }
  1102â†’            }
  1103â†’            
  1104â†’            // Update navigation highlighting if section changed
  1105â†’            if (activeSection && activeSection.id !== lastActiveSection) {
  1106â†’                // ONLY remove active state from corporate sub-navigation links, not main nav
  1107â†’                navList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(link => {
  1108â†’                    link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
  1109â†’                });
  1110â†’                
  1111â†’                // Add active state to current section's nav link
  1112â†’                const activeLink = navList.querySelector(`a[href="#${activeSection.id}"]`);
  1113â†’                if (activeLink) {
  1114â†’                    activeLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1115â†’                    console.log(`ğŸ” Corporate active section: ${activeSection.title}`);
  1116â†’                }
  1117â†’                
  1118â†’                lastActiveSection = activeSection.id;
  1119â†’            }
  1120â†’            
  1121â†’            ticking = false;
  1122â†’        }
  1123â†’        
  1124â†’        function onScroll() {
  1125â†’            if (!ticking) {
  1126â†’                requestAnimationFrame(updateActiveNavigation);
  1127â†’                ticking = true;
  1128â†’            }
  1129â†’        }
  1130â†’        
  1131â†’        // Clean up any existing scroll listeners for corporate content
  1132â†’        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
  1133â†’            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
  1134â†’        }
  1135â†’        
  1136â†’        // Set up scroll listener for corporate content
  1137â†’        window.corporateScrollListener = onScroll;
  1138â†’        window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
  1139â†’        console.log('âœ… Corporate scroll listener activated');
  1140â†’        
  1141â†’        // Initial check
  1142â†’        updateActiveNavigation();
  1143â†’        
  1144â†’        console.log('âœ… Corporate content scroll spy setup complete');
  1145â†’    }
  1146â†’
  1147â†’    function fixSidebarStylingConflicts() {
  1148â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Fixing sidebar styling conflicts...');
  1149â†’        
  1150â†’        // Ensure sidebar scrolling works properly
  1151â†’        const sidebar = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary .md-sidebar__scrollwrap');
  1152â†’        if (sidebar) {
  1153â†’            sidebar.style.overflowY = 'auto';
  1154â†’            sidebar.style.height = 'calc(100vh - 2.4rem)';
  1155â†’        }
  1156â†’        
  1157â†’        // Fix potential z-index conflicts
  1158â†’        const sidebarContainer = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary');
  1159â†’        if (sidebarContainer) {
  1160â†’            sidebarContainer.style.zIndex = '3';
  1161â†’        }
  1162â†’        
  1163â†’        // Ensure bottom navigation doesn't overlap
  1164â†’        const bottomNav = document.querySelector('.md-footer');
  1165â†’        if (bottomNav) {
  1166â†’            bottomNav.style.position = 'relative';
  1167â†’            bottomNav.style.zIndex = '1';
  1168â†’        }
  1169â†’        
  1170â†’        // Fix any content overflow issues
  1171â†’        const contentArea = document.querySelector('.md-content');
  1172â†’        if (contentArea) {
  1173â†’            contentArea.style.overflow = 'visible';
  1174â†’        }
  1175â†’        
  1176â†’        console.log('âœ… Sidebar styling conflicts fixed');
  1177â†’    }

  1179â†’    function hidePublicNavigationItems() {

  1182â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();

  1185â†’                linkText.includes('Local Development Environment Setup') ||
  1186â†’                linkText.includes('Local Setup Requirements') ||
  1187â†’                linkText.includes('Setup Steps') ||
  1188â†’                linkText.includes('OpenAI Setup') ||
  1189â†’                linkText.includes('Anthropic Claude Setup') ||
  1190â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Setup') ||
  1191â†’                linkText.includes('Local LLM Options')) {
  1192â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1193â†’                if (listItem) {
  1194â†’                    console.log('Hiding public nav item:', linkText);
  1195â†’                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
  1196â†’                }
  1197â†’            }
  1198â†’        });
  1199â†’    }

### Assistant

Perfect! Now I can see the issue. The network detection script has a global variable `isCorporateNetworkDetected` that tracks the corporate network status, but the corporate content loader is not checking this variable before loading content.

The key issue is that the corporate content loader's auto-loading logic in the `DOMContentLoaded` event handler (lines 884-904 in corporate-content-loader.js) doesn't respect the network detection results. It just checks if the page needs corporate content and then loads it regardless of network status.

Let me fix this by modifying the corporate content loader to respect the network detection:

### Assistant

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{

  "new_string": "    // Auto-load corporate content when needed and authorized\n    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {\n        console.log('ğŸ” Corporate content loader initialized');\n        \n        // Check if current page needs corporate content\n        if (window.CorporateContentLoader.isCorporateContentNeeded()) {\n            console.log('ğŸ” Page needs corporate content, checking network authorization...');\n            \n            // Wait a bit for network detection to complete\n            setTimeout(async () => {\n                // Check if network detection has authorized corporate content access\n                // This checks the global variable set by network-detection.js\n                const isAuthorized = window.isCorporateNetworkDetected || \n                                   (typeof isCorporateNetworkDetected !== 'undefined' && isCorporateNetworkDetected);\n                \n                if (isAuthorized) {\n                    console.log('âœ… Corporate network detected - loading corporate content');\n                    try {\n                        const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();\n                        if (loaded) {\n                            console.log('âœ… Corporate content loaded successfully');\n                        } else {\n                            console.log('âŒ Corporate content loading failed or content not available');\n                        }\n                    } catch (error) {\n                        console.error('âŒ Error loading corporate content:', error);\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    console.log('ğŸŒ Public network detected - skipping corporate content');\n                }\n            }, 2000); // Wait 2 seconds for network detection to complete\n        } else {\n            console.log('ğŸ” Page does not need corporate content');\n        }"

### Assistant

Excellent! The push was successful. Now let me provide a summary of the fix:

## âœ… Fixed: Corporate Content Loading Issue

I've successfully fixed the issue where corporate content was being displayed even when users were on public networks. Here's what was wrong and how I fixed it:

### The Problem
The corporate content loader was auto-loading corporate content without checking if the network detection had authorized access. This caused BMW-specific content to appear even when the network detection correctly identified that the user was on a public network.

### The Solution
1. **Network Detection Integration**: Modified the corporate content loader to check the global `isCorporateNetworkDetected` variable set by the network detection script
2. **Timing Coordination**: Added a 2-second delay to allow network detection to complete before checking authorization
3. **Authorization Check**: Corporate content now only loads when network detection confirms BMW corporate network access

### Key Changes Made
- **`corporate-content-loader.js`**: Updated the auto-loading logic to respect network detection results
- **Cache buster**: Updated timestamp to `2025-09-21T08:45:00Z` to force browser refresh
- **`main.html`**: Updated cache buster in template

### How It Works Now
1. Page loads and both scripts initialize
2. Network detection runs and determines if user is on BMW corporate network
3. Corporate content loader waits 2 seconds for network detection to complete
4. If authorized (corporate network), loads and displays corporate content
5. If not authorized (public network), skips corporate content loading

The fix has been committed and pushed to GitHub. The GitHub Pages deployment will automatically update the published site with this fix, ensuring that corporate content only appears for users actually on the BMW corporate network.
